# Orphan call edges (741 callees, 390 with a real-body caller)

Retail calls these functions, but the reconstructed caller emits no such call in our LLVM IR - the caller is a stub/@early-stop or fakes the call via a view/raw-offset. Each missing call reloc caps the caller's %. **[real]** = the caller is a matched body (not a src/Stub/ stub) that emits other calls but not this one - fix these first.
